Excited for this concept of this style of CGI going popular. I believe it has a ton of potential, not necessarily for it being used only to adapt existing IP's but to make new IP's using this format. It really can provide unlimited creative freedom in the same way anime does for example. The scope, scale, possibilities are endless compared to a normal production imo (tho I might be wrong since I'm no filmmaker) even the characters are not limited to what the pool of actors you have, since you can create them from scratch exactly how you envision them. Despite there being multiple attempts (like the Final Fantasy movies, GantzO) I think something with better direction, script and overall quality can provide the push the medium needs for it to be taken seriously other than the incredible cinematics for videogames like The Old Republic or Warcraft. Even it might become a better alternative to adapt anime instead of going full live action ğŸ‘€

I'm the only one that thinks that this looks bad? Maybe I'm just being pessimistic. But why do I get the sensation that this isn't an anthology of stories based on those universes, and more of a "Ready Player One" referential mash-up? I get is an anthology, but at the same time I get the sensation that the connective tissue isn't going to be just stories of these characters from different universes. But something more like "player character hops into virtual reality, and has to personify the protagonists of different franchises to advance through each level". I feel like this bit at 0:49 of Kratos in a modern city adds towards my suspicions. It's not going to be a small chapter of Kratos during his journey to become a better person. It's going to be "oh, shit, we have all these weird videogame characters going through places like New York, or a weird sci-fi space town. How wacky is that?".
